SELECT c."Id", c."CoverageName", c."Latitude", c."Lga", c."Longitude", c."State"
FROM "CoverageLocations" AS c
WHERE EXISTS (
    SELECT 1
    FROM unnest(@__locationWords_0) AS l(value)
    WHERE (l.value IS NOT NULL AND strpos(lower(c."CoverageName"), l.value) > 0) OR (l.value IS NOT NULL AND strpos(lower(c."Lga"), l.value) > 0) OR (l.value IS NOT NULL AND strpos(lower(c."State"), l.value) > 0))
